(iii) sabhu khan pharen sementt kaanikrett je bunyaad te, jeko sanot men aen khharo chhadiyo windo aahe, gharubl tholhh je amk waryun ptl (Brass), ttame(Copper), jsata (Zinc), sheshe (Glass), yaa bdre nambaru (Zero number) je blorn je chwari je thhil pten saan hiku kara, shnra aen gharubl dzain jaa khanua thuhea wajan. (iv) gharubl tinasb je hisaab saan map waryun peten zariay sementt aen blor je ttkarn khe pharen skul haalat men kanhin saafu pke frshe ttkare te para koshish kare tgarea yaa biay kanhin ahdre thunao (Container) men ojhi thoro thoro paani milaie aetre ghattunu (Workability) taaen beharje jetre men iho istaemal karanu je laiq banje, poi inahia khe khanun andar luhe tartib saan lohh je karnea zariay pthaare thphkayun dei gteo waji.
